| 1:15:14| First, in 1975 when I bought the house.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4514)|

| 1:15:25| And the third time in 2004 when the metal pipe rusted out again and had to be replaced at taxpayer expense.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4525)|
| 1:15:33| The 1989 pipe failure also impacted the county's pavement management program.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4533)|
| 1:15:41| The replacement of the pipe required excavating new asphalt on Chaliford Road,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4541)|
| 1:15:46| which had recently been repaved.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4546)|
| 1:15:49| I contend if concrete pipe had been used under the road when the subdivision was developed,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4549)|
| 1:15:54| I and my neighbors would not be driving over a bump in the road for the past 18 years.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4554)|
| 1:16:00| I keep hearing that flexibility to allow other types of pipe under roads besides concrete will help home buyers afford a house.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4560)|
| 1:16:09| I do not believe this can be proven when you put pencil to paper.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4569)|
| 1:16:13| Those who offer this argument say it loud and often and hope that when they say it loud and often,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4573)|
| 1:16:19| then somehow it will become the truth.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4579)|
| 1:16:22| But the truth is that in real life conditions in Knox County,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4582)|
| 1:16:26| and specifically in Berkshire Woods subdivision where I live,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4586)|
| 1:16:30| the metal pipe under Chaliford Road has failed two times in 45 years.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4590)|
| 1:16:36| And as you can see from the picture that I passed around and I sent to you in the mail,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4596)|
| 1:16:42| the pipe is currently rusting on the bottom and is destined to again fail soon for the third time.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4602)|
| 1:16:49| The truth is any savings in house price is offset by taxes to pay for the pipe maintenance.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4609)|
| 1:16:56| Flexibility in the choice of pipe materials under Chaliford Road has not saved the taxpayers one penny.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4616)|
| 1:17:04| Let me speak now as a civil engineer.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4624)|
| 1:17:07| In my 16 plus years as engineering director for the city of Knoxville,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4627)|
| 1:17:12| time and time again we wrote work orders to the public service department to remove rusted out metal pipe under roads| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4632)|
| 1:17:20| and replace them with concrete pipe.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4640)|
| 1:17:23| Also in my role as engineering director,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4643)|
| 1:17:26| I recommended to city council that they authorize and fund construction contracts to replace failed stone culverts| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4646)|
| 1:17:34| and rusted out metal pipes.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4654)|
| 1:17:37| Example locations that I recall were on Cecil Avenue, Jackson at Willow,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4657)|
| 1:17:43| locations in West Hills, Overbrook and Hedge Apple in South Knoxville,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4663)|
| 1:17:48| and how can anyone not recall Paper Mill Road?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4668)|
| 1:17:52| Yet after 16 years, I do not recall one time that a work order was sent to the public service department| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4672)|
| 1:17:59| or that I made the recommendation to city council to replace a failed concrete pipe under a public roadway.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4679)|
| 1:18:07| In fact, I've seen concrete pipe carrying stormwater in Sequoia Hill subdivision that has been in place for almost 100 years| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4687)|
| 1:18:14| and still functions properly.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4694)|
| 1:18:17| In closing, I will address the stormwater ordinance as an educator.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4697)|
| 1:18:22| Since my retirement as Knoxville's director of engineering,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4702)|
| 1:18:25| I've taught a graduate level class at the University of Tennessee| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4705)|
| 1:18:28| in the Department of Civil and Environmental Engineering.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4708)|
| 1:18:31| The name of the class is Urban Systems Engineering Management.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4711)|
| 1:18:35| Some of those who take the class aspire to be city and county engineers,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4715)|
| 1:18:39| public works directors and city managers.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4719)|
| 1:18:43| One of the topics in the class is the police power that local government legislative bodies have| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4723)|
| 1:18:49| to pass ordinances to ensure orderly growth and development.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4729)|
| 1:18:54| I point out to my students that as public works professionals,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4734)|
| 1:18:58| they will be making recommendations to legislative bodies concerning ordinances| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4738)|
| 1:19:02| that provide for the public's safety, health and welfare.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4742)|
| 1:19:07| An example I give them relating to the value of the ordinances| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4747)|
| 1:19:12| is one of the earliest ordinances put in place by local government in the United States.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4752)|
| 1:19:18| This ordinance was enacted in Savannah, Georgia, more than two centuries ago.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4758)|
| 1:19:23| In 1759, 248 years ago to be exact.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4763)|
| 1:19:28| At the time, some home builders were building houses with wood chimneys.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4768)|
| 1:19:32| After a period of use, the wood in the chimneys caught fire and burned the house to the ground.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4772)|
| 1:19:39| Not only did one house burn to the ground, but whole blocks of houses would burn to the ground| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4779)|
| 1:19:44| because of one chimney made of materials inadequate for that particular application.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4784)|
| 1:19:50| After the wood chimney fires, Savannah's General Assembly decided for the safety, health and welfare| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4790)|
| 1:19:56| of the entire community to put in place an ordinance requiring permanent chimney materials| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4796)|
| 1:20:02| that could withstand fire and heat.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4802)|
| 1:20:04| And the ordinance went as far as to prohibit home builder construction| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4804)|
| 1:20:08| and even repair of wooden chimneys.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4808)|
| 1:20:12| This example I give my students about the value and importance of ordinances| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4812)|
| 1:20:17| applies perfectly here today with the proposed Knox County Stormwater Ordinance| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4817)|
| 1:20:24| and the requirement of concrete pipe materials in three critical areas.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4824)|
| 1:20:31| As originally written, this ordinance allows for the property owner to use whatever material they choose| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4831)|
| 1:20:37| as long as there's no detrimental impact on the public's safety, health and welfare.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4837)|
| 1:20:43| As written, the section of the ordinance requiring reinforced concrete pipe| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4843)|
| 1:20:48| and three critical and limited applications is logical, responsible,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4848)|
| 1:20:53| and what is best for Knox County taxpayers and for quality growth.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=4853)|

| 2:18:29| Clerk, if you'll read it into the record.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8309)|
| 2:18:33| Whereas on July the 19th, 2007, noted businessman Allen Gill passed away at the age of 86,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8313)|
| 2:18:40| and whereas Mr. Gill was survived by his loving wife of 64 years, Hilda,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8320)|
| 2:18:45| his daughter and son-in-law Laura and Larry Bailey, four grandchildren and eight great-grandchildren,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8325)|
| 2:18:52| and whereas Allen Gill was a faithful member of First Baptist Church of Powell where he was a deacon and greeter,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8332)|
| 2:18:58| and whereas Mr. Gill commendably served his country as a sergeant in the 592nd AAF base unit during the World War II,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8338)|
| 2:19:12| and whereas Mr. Gill worked as a general manager for the Hossdale Powell Utility District for 45 years,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8352)|
| 2:19:18| and whereas Mr. Gill was a member of many professional and civic organizations,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8358)|
| 2:19:22| which include being a charter member and past president of Powell Lines Club,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8362)|
| 2:19:27| member and past president of Hoss Business and Professional Club,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8367)|
| 2:19:31| charter member of Powell Business and Professional Association,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8371)|
| 2:19:35| honorary life member of Tennessee Water and Wastewater Association,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8375)|
| 2:19:39| and past chairman and lifetime member of American Water Works Association.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8379)|
| 2:19:45| Whereas among his many awards and achievements, Allen Gill was named the 1985 Powell Businessman of the Year,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8385)|
| 2:19:52| received the 1992 Man of the Year Award by the Hoss Business and Professional Club,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8392)|
| 2:19:57| the 1992 Powell Lines Club Merit Award,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8397)|
| 2:20:02| and the 1988 Hall of Fame for Water and Wastewater Professionals.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8402)|
| 2:20:07| And whereas Allen Gill was recently honored by the Tennessee Association of Utility Districts| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8407)|
| 2:20:12| at their 50th anniversary celebration,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8412)|
| 2:20:15| as he was a founder of the organization that now represents 184 utility districts statewide.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8415)|
| 2:20:23| And whereas in recognizing Mr. Gill, the TAUD leadership said,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8423)|
| 2:20:28| TAUD and the state of Tennessee are very fortunate to have men of Allen Gill's integrity| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8428)|
| 2:20:34| to donate so much of their time and effort for the success of this association.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8434)|
| 2:20:39| His dedication is the personification of the spirit of all utility members across their state| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8439)|
| 2:20:46| and a role model for those new members entering the utility field.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8446)|
| 2:20:50| And whereas the Knox County Commission wishes to express its appreciation of Allen Gill's many contributions| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8450)|
| 2:20:56| and service to the Powell community and all of Knox County.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=8456)|

| 2:33:07| It's 422.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9187)|
| 2:33:11| My name is Jim Golden.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9191)|
| 2:33:12| I live at 4139 Skyline Drive in an old home frequently vandalized by gangs| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9192)|
| 2:33:19| because children hide in my yard after they get off a school bus from these gangs.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9199)|
| 2:33:27| I was born during World War II.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9207)|
| 2:33:32| My grandmother had been an officer stationed here in support of the war effort| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9212)|
| 2:33:36| where she met and married my father, who was with the Knoxville Journal at the time.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9216)|
| 2:33:40| In my youth, I attended YMCA, was a safety patrol at Holston Junior Senior High School,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9220)|
| 2:33:50| was a route delivery boy for the Knoxville New Sentinel,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9230)|
| 2:33:53| balanced automobile tires and learned to straighten frames and line front ends in my uncle's shop,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9233)|
| 2:34:00| raced in the American Soapbox Derby when you had to design and build your own car,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9240)|
| 2:34:06| swam on Knoxville's first swim team,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9246)|
| 2:34:09| took the first black motorcycle rider to the highway patrol to get his license, first youth.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9249)|
| 2:34:17| I worked after school in a boat repair shop owned by my algebra teacher.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9257)|
| 2:34:23| I began learning the tool and die trade at Hanchard Machine Company,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9263)|
| 2:34:27| sold street rods with older boys, one at Seabury's Garage in the Five Points area,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9267)|
| 2:34:33| worked secretly for Homelite Chainsaw Company because I was underage| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9273)|
| 2:34:37| and they couldn't tell the company that I worked there.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9277)|
| 2:34:40| I also worked at JFG Coffee Company later and learned every job in every department.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9280)|
| 2:34:48| I worked at Burkhart's Esso my senior year.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9288)|
| 2:34:52| And after high school, I took an extra job in South Carolina building lake homes| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9292)|
| 2:35:00| and started what became one of the largest marinas, sank the first pylons for that.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9300)|
| 2:35:09| I served as a nuclear missile technician in the Strategic Air Command of the United States Air Force during Vietnam,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9309)|
| 2:35:19| where I also attended the University of Wyoming and later here at the University of Tennessee.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9319)|
| 2:35:24| I served in the engineering department for American Telephone Telegraph Company across America| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9324)|
| 2:35:30| and later retired from South Central Bell here.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9330)|
| 2:35:34| I've operated a small company called Golden Research since high school,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9334)|
| 2:35:38| where I back up large corporations in development of new methods and technologies,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9338)|
| 2:35:43| mostly where others have failed in fields of aeronautics, combustion, solar energy, and medical community.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom070827part1?start=9343)|
